     1→# BMW Corporate Content Repository
     2→
     3→This repository contains BMW-specific corporate content for the Agentic AI Nano Degree course, featuring advanced corporate network (CN) detection and encrypted content delivery.
     4→
     5→## Overview
     6→
     7→The BMW Corporate Content system provides secure, network-aware content delivery that automatically detects corporate network access and serves appropriate content based on the user's network environment.
     8→
     9→## Corporate Network (CN) Detection System
    10→
    11→### How CN Detection Works
    12→
    13→The system uses a multi-layered approach to detect BMW corporate network access:
    14→
    15→```mermaid
    16→graph TD
    17→    A[Page Load] --> B[Initialize Network Detection]
    18→    B --> C[Check Hostname Patterns]
    19→    C --> D{Corporate Domain?}
    20→    D -->|Yes| E[Show Corporate Content]
    21→    D -->|No| F[Check External IP]
    22→    F --> G{BMW IP Range?}
    23→    G -->|Yes| E
    24→    G -->|No| H[Try Internal Service Check]
    25→    H --> I{ContentHub Reachable?}
    26→    I -->|Yes| E
    27→    I -->|No| J[Show Public Content]
    28→    E --> K[Load Encrypted Corporate Content]
    29→    J --> L[Load Public Content]
    30→```
    31→
    32→### Detection Methods
    33→
    34→#### 1. Hostname-Based Detection
    35→- **BMW Corporate Domains**: `*.bmw.com`, `*.bmwgroup.com`
    36→- **Internal IP Ranges**: `10.*`, `192.168.*`, `172.16-31.*`
    37→- **Development**: `localhost`, `127.0.0.1` (with fallback CN detection)
    38→
    39→#### 2. External IP Range Detection
    40→- **Primary BMW Range**: `160.46.*` (verified working range)
    41→- **Additional Ranges**: `194.114.*`, `195.34.*`, `212.204.*`
    42→- **Method**: Uses `api.ipify.org` to determine external IP
    43→
    44→#### 3. Internal Service Accessibility
    45→- **Target**: `https://contenthub.bmwgroup.net/favicon.ico`
    46→- **Method**: Image load test with timeout
    47→- **Timeout**: 2 seconds maximum
    48→- **Fallback**: Public content if unreachable
    49→
    50→### Network Detection Flow
    51→
    52→```mermaid
    53→sequenceDiagram
    54→    participant U as User Browser
    55→    participant ND as Network Detection
    56→    participant IP as IP API Service
    57→    participant CH as ContentHub
    58→    participant CC as Corporate Content
    59→    
    60→    U->>ND: Page Load
    61→    ND->>ND: Check Hostname
    62→    alt Corporate Domain
    63→        ND->>CC: Load Corporate Content
    64→    else Public Domain
    65→        ND->>IP: Get External IP
    66→        IP-->>ND: IP Address
    67→        alt BMW IP Range
    68→            ND->>CC: Load Corporate Content
    69→        else Non-BMW IP
    70→            ND->>CH: Test Internal Access
    71→            alt ContentHub Reachable
    72→                CH-->>ND: Success
    73→                ND->>CC: Load Corporate Content
    74→            else ContentHub Unreachable
    75→                CH-->>ND: Timeout/Error
    76→                ND->>U: Show Public Content
    77→            end
    78→        end
    79→    end
    80→```
    81→
    82→## Encrypted Content System
    83→
    84→### Encryption Architecture
    85→
    86→The corporate content uses AES-GCM encryption with the following architecture:
    87→
    88→```mermaid
    89→graph LR
    90→    A[Corporate Content] --> B[AES-GCM Encryption]
    91→    B --> C[Base64 Encoding]
    92→    C --> D[JSON Manifest]
    93→    D --> E[GitHub Pages Deployment]
    94→    E --> F[Corporate Network Detection]
    95→    F --> G[Client-Side Decryption]
    96→    G --> H[Content Injection]
    97→```
    98→
    99→### Encryption Details
   100→
   101→- **Algorithm**: AES-GCM (256-bit)
   102→- **Key Derivation**: SHA-256 hash of corporate passphrase
   103→- **Authentication**: Built-in auth tag for integrity verification
   104→- **Format**: Base64-encoded JSON with IV, encrypted data, and auth tag
   105→
   106→### Content Structure
   107→
   108→```mermaid
   109→graph TD
   110→    A[content.encrypted.json] --> B[File Manifest]
   111→    A --> C[Encrypted Content Map]
   112→    C --> D[Session 10 MD Files]
   113→    C --> E[Corporate Images]
   114→    C --> F[PlantUML Diagrams]
   115→    B --> G[File Paths Array]
   116→    B --> H[Encryption Metadata]
   117→```

   141→## Deployment Architecture
   142→
   143→### GitHub Actions Workflow
   144→
   145→The corporate content is deployed through a sophisticated GitHub Actions workflow:
   146→
   147→```mermaid
   148→graph TD
   149→    A[Push to main] --> B[GitHub Actions Trigger]
   150→    B --> C[Checkout Public Repo]
   151→    C --> D[Clone Corporate Repo with PAT]
   152→    D --> E[Verify Corporate Content]
   153→    E --> F[Build MkDocs Site]
   154→    F --> G[Copy Corporate Content to Build]
   155→    G --> H[Create .nojekyll File]
   156→    H --> I[Deploy to GitHub Pages]
   157→```
   158→
   159→### Key Features
   160→
   161→- **Private Repository Integration**: Uses Personal Access Token (PAT) to access private corporate content
   162→- **Jekyll Bypass**: Creates `.nojekyll` file to prevent GitHub Pages from filtering corporate directories
   163→- **Content Verification**: Validates encrypted content structure before deployment
   164→- **Secure Copy**: Copies encrypted content to final site build without exposing source
   165→
   166→## Content Access Control
   167→
   168→### Network-Based Access
   169→
   170→```mermaid
   171→graph TD
   172→    A[User Access Request] --> B{Network Detection}
   173→    B -->|Corporate Network| C[Show Corporate Navigation]
   174→    B -->|Public Network| D[Hide Corporate Navigation]
   175→    C --> E[Load Encrypted Content]
   176→    C --> F[Show Session 10 Link]
   177→    C --> G[Enable Corporate Features]
   178→    D --> H[Show Public Content Only]
   179→    D --> I[Hide Session 10]
   180→    E --> J[Decrypt with Corporate Key]
   181→    J --> K[Inject Corporate Content]
   182→```

   129→## Corporate Content Management
   130→
   131→This repository implements a sophisticated content management system that supports both public and corporate-specific content:
   132→
   133→### Repository Access Models
   134→
   135→**Public Access (Standard Clone):**
   136→- Public users clone the repository without corporate content
   137→- Receives generic course materials suitable for general audiences
   138→- No access to corporate-specific content or proprietary configurations
   139→
   140→**Corporate Access (Submodule Clone):**
   141→- Corporate users clone with `--recurse-submodules` to access additional content
   142→- Includes corporate-specific examples, configurations, and deployment guides
   143→- Corporate content stored in a separate private repository as a git submodule
   144→
   145→### Architecture Overview
   146→
   147→**Dual Content System:**
   148→- **Public Content**: Generic course materials available to all users
   149→- **Corporate Content**: Organization-specific content accessible only to authorized users
   150→
   151→**Key Components:**
   152→- **Private Submodule**: Corporate content stored in private repository (`docs-content/corporate-only/`)
   153→- **Network Detection**: Automatic corporate network detection (`docs-content/javascripts/network-detection.js`)
   154→- **Content Encryption**: Corporate content encrypted for secure public deployment (`scripts/encrypt-corporate-content.js`)
   155→- **Dynamic Decryption**: Client-side decryption when accessed from corporate network (`docs-content/javascripts/corporate-content-loader.js`)
   156→
   157→### Content Structure
   158→
   159→```
   160→nano-degree/
   161→├── docs-content/
   162→│   ├── corporate-only/              # Private submodule (corporate users only)
   163→│   │   ├── 00_intro/coder-detailed.md    # Corporate environment details
   164→│   │   ├── 03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10*    # Corporate enterprise deployment
   165→│   │   ├── images/corp-*.png            # Corporate-specific diagrams
   166→│   │   ├── puml/corp-*.puml             # Corporate architecture diagrams
   167→│   │   ├── content.encrypted.json       # Encrypted content manifest
   168→│   │   └── test.encrypted.json          # Decryption test file
   169→│   ├── 00_intro/coder.md            # Conditional content (corporate/public)
   170→│   └── javascripts/
   171→│       ├── network-detection.js      # Corporate network detection
   172→│       └── corporate-content-loader.js # Content decryption system
   173→└── scripts/encrypt-corporate-content.js # Encryption utility
   174→```
   175→
   176→### Content Publishing Workflow
   177→
   178→**For Public Deployment:**
   179→1. Corporate content encrypted using AES-256-GCM
   180→2. Encrypted manifest included in public repository
   181→3. Network detection determines content visibility
   182→4. Corporate content decrypted client-side on corporate network
   183→
   184→**For Corporate Environment:**
   185→- Direct access to unencrypted corporate content
   186→- Corporate cloud development environment
   187→- Pre-configured templates and organization-specific integrations
   188→
   189→### Development Workflow
   190→
   191→**Managing Corporate Content:**
   192→```bash
   193→# Update corporate content
   194→cd docs-content/corporate-only
   195→# Make changes to corporate files
   196→git add . && git commit -m "Update corporate content"
   197→git push origin main
   198→
   199→# Encrypt for public deployment
   200→node scripts/encrypt-corporate-content.js
   201→
   202→# Test decryption (corporate network only)
   203→# Access from corporate network - decryption tested automatically
   204→```
   205→
   206→**Content Guidelines:**
   207→- Use conditional divs: `<div class="corp-corporate-only">` and `<div class="corp-public-alternative">`
   208→- Corporate images: Store in `corporate-only/images/` with relative paths
   209→- Reference corporate content: Use `../corporate-only/` paths from public content
   210→
   211→### Security Features
   212→
   213→- **Network-based Access Control**: Content visibility based on corporate network detection
   214→- **Encryption at Rest**: Corporate content encrypted when included in public repository
   215→- **Client-side Decryption**: Secure decryption only available from corporate network
   216→- **IP Range Validation**: Multiple corporate IP range patterns for network detection
   217→- **Automatic Content Switching**: Seamless transition between corporate and public content
   218→
   219→This system ensures corporate-specific content remains secure while allowing flexible deployment across both internal and public environments.
   220→
